\int{{{\left(x + 4\right)}^{4}}\cdot{e^{\left(4 \, x\right)}}\;dx} = \answer{{\frac{1}{128} \, {\left(32 \, x^{4} - 32 \, x^{3} + 24 \, x^{2} - 12 \, x + 3\right)} e^{\left(4 \, x\right)} + \frac{1}{8} \, {\left(32 \, x^{3} - 24 \, x^{2} + 12 \, x - 3\right)} e^{\left(4 \, x\right)} + 3 \, {\left(8 \, x^{2} - 4 \, x + 1\right)} e^{\left(4 \, x\right)} + 16 \, {\left(4 \, x - 1\right)} e^{\left(4 \, x\right)} + 64 \, e^{\left(4 \, x\right)}}+C}
\]
\end{problem}}%}
